lemma ReverseLength<T>(s: seq<T>)
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    // Base case
  } else {
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s)| == |reverse(s[1..])| + 1;
  }
}

lemma ReverseReverse<T>(s: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(s)) == s
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    // Base case
  } else {
    ReverseReverse(s[1..]);
    ReverseAppend(reverse(s[1..]), [s[0]]);
    assert reverse(reverse(s)) == s;
  }
}

lemma ReverseAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
// Inductive proof using rule induction
    // following function: reverse
    if (|s1| == 0) {
    } else {
        ReverseAppend(s1[1..], s2);
        assert s1 == [s1[0]] + s1[1..];
        assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
        assert reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2));
        assert reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2)) == reverse(s1[1..] + s2) + [s1[0]];
        assert reverse(s1[1..] + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..]);
        assert reverse(s1) == reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]];
        SeqAssoc(reverse(s2), reverse(s1[1..]), [s1[0]]);
    }
}

lemma ReverseFirst<T>(s: seq<T>)
  requires |s| > 0
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
  ensures reverse(s)[|reverse(s)| - 1] == s[0]
  ensures reverse(s)[0] == s[|s| - 1]
{
  ReverseLength(s);
  if |s| == 1 {
    assert reverse(s) == [s[0]];
  } else {
    ReverseFirst(s[1..]);
    assert reverse(s) == reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]];
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s[1..])| == |s| - 1;
  }
}

lemma SeqAssoc<T>(a: seq<T>, b: seq<T>, c: seq<T>)
  ensures a + (b + c) == (a + b) + c
{
  // Dafny proves this automatically
}

lemma QueueSizeProperty<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  ensures queueSize(q) == |queueToSeq(q)|
{
  ReverseLength(q.rear);
}

lemma EnqueueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>, x: T)
  ensures queueToSeq(enqueue(q, x)) == queueToSeq(q) + [x]
  ensures queueSize(enqueue(q, x)) == queueSize(q) + 1
{
  var q' := enqueue(q, x);
  assert q'.front == q.front;
  assert q'.rear == [x] + q.rear;

  ReverseAppend([x], q.rear);
  assert reverse([x]) == [x];
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + reverse([x]);
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + [x];

  calc == {
    queueToSeq(q');
    q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
    q.front + reverse([x] + q.rear);
    q.front + (reverse(q.rear) + [x]);
    { SeqAssoc(q.front, reverse(q.rear), [x]); }
    (q.front + reverse(q.rear)) + [x];
    queueToSeq(q) + [x];
  }

  QueueSizeProperty(q);
  QueueSizeProperty(q');
}

lemma DequeueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures |queueToSeq(q)| > 0
  ensures queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
  ensures queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
{
  if |q.front| > 0 {
    assert queueToSeq(q) == q.front + reverse(q.rear);
    assert queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == q.front[1..] + reverse(q.rear);
    assert queueFront(q) == q.front[0];
  } else {
    assert q.front == [];
    assert |q.rear| > 0;
    var rev := reverse(q.rear);
    ReverseLength(q.rear);
    assert |rev| == |q.rear|;
    assert queueToSeq(q) == rev;
    assert queueFront(q) == q.rear[|q.rear| - 1];

    ReverseFirst(q.rear);
    assert rev[0] == q.rear[|q.rear| - 1];

    if |q.rear| == 1 {
      assert rev == [q.rear[0]];
      assert queueToSeq(q) == [q.rear[0]];
      assert queueFront(q) == q.rear[0];
      assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == q.rear[0];
    } else {
      assert |rev| > 1;
      assert queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == rev[1..];
      assert queueFront(q) == rev[0];
    }
  }
}

lemma SimpleQueueEquivalence<T>(sq: SimpleQueue<T>, q: Queue<T>)
  requires sq.elements == queueToSeq(q)
  ensures simpleQueueIsEmpty(sq) == queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures simpleQueueSize(sq) == queueSize(q)
{
  if queueIsEmpty(q) {
    assert q.front == [] && q.rear == [];
    assert queueToSeq(q) == [];
    assert sq.elements == [];
  }
  QueueSizeProperty(q);
}

// Queue operations: enqueue, dequeue, isEmpty, size

datatype Queue<T> = Queue(front: seq<T>, rear: seq<T>)

function {:spec} queueEmpty<T>(): Queue<T>
{
  Queue([], [])
}

predicate {:spec} queueIsEmpty<T>(q: Queue<T>)
{
  q.front == [] && q.rear == []
}

function {:spec} enqueue<T>(q: Queue<T>, x: T): Queue<T>
{
  Queue(q.front, [x] + q.rear)
}

function {:spec} dequeue<T>(q: Queue<T>): Queue<T>
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
{
  if |q.front| > 0 then
    Queue(q.front[1..], q.rear)
  else
    // Front is empty, so we reverse rear and put it in front
    if |q.rear| == 1 then
      Queue([], [])
    else
      Queue(reverse(q.rear)[1..], [])
}

function {:spec} queueFront<T>(q: Queue<T>): T
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
{
  if |q.front| > 0 then
    q.front[0]
  else
    // Front is empty, so the front element is the first element of rear (when reversed)
    q.rear[|q.rear| - 1]
}

function {:spec} queueSize<T>(q: Queue<T>): nat
{
  |q.front| + |q.rear|
}

function {:spec} queueToSeq<T>(q: Queue<T>): seq<T>
{
  q.front + reverse(q.rear)
}

function reverse<T>(s: seq<T>): seq<T>
{
  if |s| == 0 then []
  else reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]]
}

lemma ReverseAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
// Inductive proof using rule induction
    // following function: reverse
    if (|s1| == 0) {
        assert s1 + s2 == s2;
        assert reverse(s1) == [];
        assert reverse(s2) + reverse(s1) == reverse(s2) + [] == reverse(s2);
        assert reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1);
    } else {
        ReverseAppend(s1[1..], s2);
        assert s1 == [s1[0]] + s1[1..];
        assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
        assert reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2));
        assert reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2)) == reverse(s1[1..] + s2) + [s1[0]];
        assert reverse(s1[1..] + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..]);
        assert reverse(s1) == reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]];
        SeqAssoc(reverse(s2), reverse(s1[1..]), [s1[0]]);
    }
}

lemma ReverseFirst<T>(s: seq<T>)
  requires |s| > 0
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
  ensures reverse(s)[|reverse(s)| - 1] == s[0]
  ensures reverse(s)[0] == s[|s| - 1]
{
  ReverseLength(s);
  if |s| == 1 {
    assert reverse(s) == [s[0]];
  } else {
    ReverseFirst(s[1..]);
    assert reverse(s) == reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]];
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s[1..])| == |s| - 1;
  }
}

{
  // Dafny proves this automatically

lemma EnqueueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>, x: T)
  ensures queueToSeq(enqueue(q, x)) == queueToSeq(q) + [x]
  ensures queueSize(enqueue(q, x)) == queueSize(q) + 1
{
  var q' := enqueue(q, x);
  assert q'.front == q.front;
  assert q'.rear == [x] + q.rear;

  ReverseAppend([x], q.rear);
  assert reverse([x]) == [x];
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + reverse([x]);
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + [x];

  calc == {
    queueToSeq(q');
    q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
    q.front + reverse([x] + q.rear);
    q.front + (reverse(q.rear) + [x]);
    { SeqAssoc(q.front, reverse(q.rear), [x]); }
    (q.front + reverse(q.rear)) + [x];
    queueToSeq(q) + [x];
  }

  QueueSizeProperty(q);
  QueueSizeProperty(q');
}

lemma DequeueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures |queueToSeq(q)| > 0
  ensures queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
  ensures queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
{
  if |q.front| > 0 {
    assert queueToSeq(q) == q.front + reverse(q.rear);
    assert queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == q.front[1..] + reverse(q.rear);
    assert queueFront(q) == q.front[0];
  } else {
    assert q.front == [];
    assert |q.rear| > 0;
    var rev := reverse(q.rear);
    ReverseLength(q.rear);
    assert |rev| == |q.rear|;
    assert queueToSeq(q) == rev;
    assert queueFront(q) == q.rear[|q.rear| - 1];

    ReverseFirst(q.rear);
    assert rev[0] == q.rear[|q.rear| - 1];

    if |q.rear| == 1 {
      assert rev == [q.rear[0]];
      assert queueToSeq(q) == [q.rear[0]];
      assert queueFront(q) == q.rear[0];
      assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == q.rear[0];
    } else {
      assert |rev| > 1;
      assert queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == rev[1..];
      assert queueFront(q) == rev[0];
    }
  }
}

    Queue(q.front[1..], q.rear)
  else
    // Front is empty, so we reverse rear and put it in front
    if |q.rear| == 1 then
      Queue([], [])
    else
      Queue(reverse(q.rear)[1..], [])
}

function {:spec} queueFront<T>(q: Queue<T>): T
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
{
  if |q.front| > 0 then
    q.front[0]
  else
    // Front is empty, so the front element is the first element of rear (when reversed)
    q.rear[|q.rear| - 1]
}

function {:spec} queueSize<T>(q: Queue<T>): nat
{
  |q.front| + |q.rear|
}

function {:spec} queueToSeq<T>(q: Queue<T>): seq<T>
{
  q.front + reverse(q.rear)
}

function reverse<T>(s: seq<T>): seq<T>
{
  if |s| == 0 then []
  else reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]]
}

// Alternative queue representation with invariant
datatype SimpleQueue<T> = SimpleQueue(elements: seq<T>)

function {:spec} simpleQueueEmpty<T>(): SimpleQueue<T>
{
  SimpleQueue([])
}

predicate {:spec} simpleQueueIsEmpty<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>)
{
  q.elements == []
}

function {:spec} simpleEnqueue<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>, x: T): SimpleQueue<T>
{
  SimpleQueue(q.elements + [x])
}

function {:spec} simpleDequeue<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>): SimpleQueue<T>
  requires !simpleQueueIsEmpty(q)
{
  SimpleQueue(q.elements[1..])
}

function {:spec} simpleQueueFront<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>): T
  requires !simpleQueueIsEmpty(q)
{
  q.elements[0]
}

function {:spec} simpleQueueSize<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>): nat
{
  |q.elements|
}

lemma ReverseLength<T>(s: seq<T>)
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    // Base case
  } else {
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s)| == |reverse(s[1..])| + 1;
  }
}

lemma ReverseReverse<T>(s: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(s)) == s
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    // Base case
  } else {
    ReverseReverse(s[1..]);
    ReverseAppend(reverse(s[1..]), [s[0]]);
    assert reverse(reverse(s)) == s;
  }
}

lemma ReverseAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
    assert reverse(s1) == [];
  } else {
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
    ReverseAppend(s1[1..], s2);
  }
}

lemma ReverseFirst<T>(s: seq<T>)
  requires |s| > 0
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
  ensures reverse(s)[|reverse(s)| - 1] == s[0]
  ensures reverse(s)[0] == s[|s| - 1]
{
  ReverseLength(s);
  if |s| == 1 {
    assert reverse(s) == [s[0]];
  } else {
    ReverseFirst(s[1..]);
    assert reverse(s) == reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]];
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s[1..])| == |s| - 1;
  }
}

lemma SeqAssoc<T>(a: seq<T>, b: seq<T>, c: seq<T>)
  ensures a + (b + c) == (a + b) + c
{
  // Dafny proves this automatically
}

lemma QueueSizeProperty<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  ensures queueSize(q) == |queueToSeq(q)|
{
  ReverseLength(q.rear);
}

lemma EnqueueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>, x: T)
  ensures queueToSeq(enqueue(q, x)) == queueToSeq(q) + [x]
  ensures queueSize(enqueue(q, x)) == queueSize(q) + 1
{
  var q' := enqueue(q, x);
  assert q'.front == q.front;
  assert q'.rear == [x] + q.rear;

  ReverseAppend([x], q.rear);
  assert reverse([x]) == [x];
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + reverse([x]);
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + [x];

  calc == {
    queueToSeq(q');
    q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
    q.front + reverse([x] + q.rear);
    q.front + (reverse(q.rear) + [x]);
    { SeqAssoc(q.front, reverse(q.rear), [x]); }
    (q.front + reverse(q.rear)) + [x];
    queueToSeq(q) + [x];
  }

  QueueSizeProperty(q);
  QueueSizeProperty(q');
}

lemma DequeueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures |queueToSeq(q)| > 0
  ensures queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
  ensures queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
{

}

  ensures simpleQueueIsEmpty(sq) == queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures simpleQueueSize(sq) == queueSize(q)
{
  if queueIsEmpty(q) {
    assert q.front == [] && q.rear == [];
    assert queueToSeq(q) == [];
    assert sq.elements == [];
  }
  QueueSizeProperty(q);
}

{
  SimpleQueue(q.elements + [x])

lemma ReverseLength<T>(s: seq<T>)
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    // Base case
  } else {
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s)| == |reverse(s[1..])| + 1;
  }
}

lemma ReverseReverse<T>(s: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(s)) == s
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    // Base case
  } else {
    ReverseReverse(s[1..]);
    ReverseAppend(reverse(s[1..]), [s[0]]);
    assert reverse(reverse(s)) == s;
  }
}

lemma ReverseAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
    assert reverse(s1) == [];
  } else {
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
    ReverseAppend(s1[1..], s2);
  }
}

lemma ReverseFirst<T>(s: seq<T>)
  requires |s| > 0
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
  ensures reverse(s)[|reverse(s)| - 1] == s[0]
  ensures reverse(s)[0] == s[|s| - 1]
{
  ReverseLength(s);
  if |s| == 1 {
    assert reverse(s) == [s[0]];
  } else {
    ReverseFirst(s[1..]);
    assert reverse(s) == reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]];
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s[1..])| == |s| - 1;
  }
}

  ensures a + (b + c) == (a + b) + c
{
  // Dafny proves this automatically
}

  ensures queueSize(q) == |queueToSeq(q)|

  ReverseLength(q.rear);

lemma EnqueueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>, x: T)
  ensures queueToSeq(enqueue(q, x)) == queueToSeq(q) + [x]
  ensures queueSize(enqueue(q, x)) == queueSize(q) + 1
{
  var q' := enqueue(q, x);
  assert q'.front == q.front;
  assert q'.rear == [x] + q.rear;

  ReverseAppend([x], q.rear);
  assert reverse([x]) == [x];
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + reverse([x]);
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + [x];

    queueToSeq(q');
    q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
    q.front + reverse([x] + q.rear);
    q.front + (reverse(q.rear) + [x]);
    { SeqAssoc(q.front, reverse(q.rear), [x]); }
    (q.front + reverse(q.rear)) + [x];
    queueToSeq(q) + [x];
  }

  QueueSizeProperty(q);
  QueueSizeProperty(q');
}

// Queue operations: enqueue, dequeue, isEmpty, size

datatype Queue<T> = Queue(front: seq<T>, rear: seq<T>)

function {:spec} queueEmpty<T>(): Queue<T>
{
  Queue([], [])
}

predicate {:spec} queueIsEmpty<T>(q: Queue<T>)
{
  q.front == [] && q.rear == []
}

function {:spec} enqueue<T>(q: Queue<T>, x: T): Queue<T>
{
  Queue(q.front, [x] + q.rear)
}

function {:spec} dequeue<T>(q: Queue<T>): Queue<T>
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
{
  if |q.front| > 0 then
    Queue(q.front[1..], q.rear)
  else
    // Front is empty, so we reverse rear and put it in front
    if |q.rear| == 1 then
      Queue([], [])
    else
      Queue(reverse(q.rear)[1..], [])
}

function {:spec} queueFront<T>(q: Queue<T>): T
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
{
  if |q.front| > 0 then
    q.front[0]
  else
    // Front is empty, so the front element is the first element of rear (when reversed)
    q.rear[|q.rear| - 1]
}

function {:spec} queueSize<T>(q: Queue<T>): nat
{
  |q.front| + |q.rear|
}

function {:spec} queueToSeq<T>(q: Queue<T>): seq<T>
{
  q.front + reverse(q.rear)
}

function reverse<T>(s: seq<T>): seq<T>
{
  if |s| == 0 then []
  else reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]]
}

lemma QueueSizeProperty<T>(q: Queue<T>)

  ReverseLength(q.rear);

lemma EnqueueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>, x: T)
  ensures queueToSeq(enqueue(q, x)) == queueToSeq(q) + [x]
  ensures queueSize(enqueue(q, x)) == queueSize(q) + 1
{
  var q' := enqueue(q, x);
  assert q'.front == q.front;
  assert q'.rear == [x] + q.rear;

  ReverseAppend([x], q.rear);
  assert reverse([x]) == [x];
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + reverse([x]);
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + [x];

  calc == {
    queueToSeq(q');
    q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
    q.front + reverse([x] + q.rear);
    q.front + (reverse(q.rear) + [x]);
    { SeqAssoc(q.front, reverse(q.rear), [x]); }
    (q.front + reverse(q.rear)) + [x];
    queueToSeq(q) + [x];
  }

  QueueSizeProperty(q);
  QueueSizeProperty(q');
}

lemma DequeueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures |queueToSeq(q)| > 0
  ensures queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
  ensures queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
{
// Structural induction on q
    match q {
        case Queue(front, rear) => {
            ReverseLength(rear);
            if |front| > 0 {
                // Case 1: front is non-empty
                assert queueToSeq(q) == front + reverse(rear);
                assert |queueToSeq(q)| == |front| + |reverse(rear)|;
                assert |queueToSeq(q)| > 0;
                
                var q' := dequeue(q);
                assert q' == Queue(front[1..], rear);
                assert queueToSeq(q') == front[1..] + reverse(rear);
                
                // Show that front[1..] + reverse(rear) == (front + reverse(rear))[1..]
                assert front + reverse(rear) == [front[0]] + (front[1..] + reverse(rear));
                assert (front + reverse(rear))[1..] == front[1..] + reverse(rear);
                
                assert queueFront(q) == front[0];
                assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == front[0];
            } else {
                // Case 2: front is empty
                assert front == [];
                assert queueToSeq(q) == [] + reverse(rear) == reverse(rear);
                assert !queueIsEmpty(q);
                assert rear != [];
                ReverseLength(rear);
                assert |reverse(rear)| == |rear|;
                assert |queueToSeq(q)| == |rear|;
                assert |queueToSeq(q)| > 0;
                
                // queueFront when front is empty
                assert queueFront(q) == rear[|rear| - 1];
                ReverseFirst(rear);
                assert reverse(rear)[0] == rear[|rear| - 1];
                assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == reverse(rear)[0] == rear[|rear| - 1];
                
                if |rear| == 1 {
                    // Dequeue results in empty queue
                    var q' := dequeue(q);
                    assert q' == Queue([], []);
                    assert queueToSeq(q') == [];
                    assert queueToSeq(q) == reverse(rear);
                    assert |reverse(rear)| == 1;
                    assert queueToSeq(q)[1..] == [];
                } else {
                    // Dequeue reverses rear and takes tail
                    var q' := dequeue(q);
                    assert q' == Queue(reverse(rear)[1..], []);
                    assert queueToSeq(q') == reverse(rear)[1..] + reverse([]);
                    assert reverse([]) == [];
                    assert queueToSeq(q') == reverse(rear)[1..];
                    assert queueToSeq(q) == reverse(rear);
                    assert queueToSeq(q)[1..] == reverse(rear)[1..];
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

lemma SimpleQueueEquivalence<T>(sq: SimpleQueue<T>, q: Queue<T>)
  requires sq.elements == queueToSeq(q)
  ensures simpleQueueIsEmpty(sq) == queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures simpleQueueSize(sq) == queueSize(q)
{
  if queueIsEmpty(q) {
    assert q.front == [] && q.rear == [];
    assert queueToSeq(q) == [];
    assert sq.elements == [];
  }
  QueueSizeProperty(q);
}

// Queue operations: enqueue, dequeue, isEmpty, size

datatype Queue<T> = Queue(front: seq<T>, rear: seq<T>)

function {:spec} queueEmpty<T>(): Queue<T>
{
  Queue([], [])
}

predicate {:spec} queueIsEmpty<T>(q: Queue<T>)
{
  q.front == [] && q.rear == []
}

function {:spec} enqueue<T>(q: Queue<T>, x: T): Queue<T>
{
  Queue(q.front, [x] + q.rear)
}

function {:spec} dequeue<T>(q: Queue<T>): Queue<T>
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
{
  if |q.front| > 0 then
    Queue(q.front[1..], q.rear)
  else
    // Front is empty, so we reverse rear and put it in front
    if |q.rear| == 1 then
      Queue([], [])
    else
      Queue(reverse(q.rear)[1..], [])
}

function {:spec} queueFront<T>(q: Queue<T>): T
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
{
  if |q.front| > 0 then
    q.front[0]
  else
    // Front is empty, so the front element is the first element of rear (when reversed)
    q.rear[|q.rear| - 1]
}

function {:spec} queueSize<T>(q: Queue<T>): nat
{
  |q.front| + |q.rear|
}

function {:spec} queueToSeq<T>(q: Queue<T>): seq<T>
{
  q.front + reverse(q.rear)
}

function reverse<T>(s: seq<T>): seq<T>
{
  if |s| == 0 then []
  else reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]]
}

// Alternative queue representation with invariant
datatype SimpleQueue<T> = SimpleQueue(elements: seq<T>)

function {:spec} simpleQueueEmpty<T>(): SimpleQueue<T>
{
  SimpleQueue([])
}

predicate {:spec} simpleQueueIsEmpty<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>)
{
  q.elements == []
}

function {:spec} simpleEnqueue<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>, x: T): SimpleQueue<T>
{
  SimpleQueue(q.elements + [x])
}

function {:spec} simpleDequeue<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>): SimpleQueue<T>
  requires !simpleQueueIsEmpty(q)
{
  SimpleQueue(q.elements[1..])
}

function {:spec} simpleQueueFront<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>): T
  requires !simpleQueueIsEmpty(q)
{
  q.elements[0]
}

function {:spec} simpleQueueSize<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>): nat
{
  |q.elements|
}

lemma ReverseLength<T>(s: seq<T>)
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    // Base case
  } else {
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s)| == |reverse(s[1..])| + 1;
  }
}

lemma ReverseReverse<T>(s: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(s)) == s
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    // Base case
  } else {
    ReverseReverse(s[1..]);
    ReverseAppend(reverse(s[1..]), [s[0]]);
    assert reverse(reverse(s)) == s;
  }
}

lemma ReverseAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
    assert reverse(s1) == [];
  } else {
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
    ReverseAppend(s1[1..], s2);
  }
}

lemma ReverseFirst<T>(s: seq<T>)
  requires |s| > 0
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
  ensures reverse(s)[|reverse(s)| - 1] == s[0]
  ensures reverse(s)[0] == s[|s| - 1]
{
  ReverseLength(s);
  if |s| == 1 {
    assert reverse(s) == [s[0]];
  } else {
    ReverseFirst(s[1..]);
    assert reverse(s) == reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]];
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s[1..])| == |s| - 1;
  }
}

lemma SeqAssoc<T>(a: seq<T>, b: seq<T>, c: seq<T>)
  ensures a + (b + c) == (a + b) + c
{
  // Dafny proves this automatically
}

lemma QueueSizeProperty<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  ensures queueSize(q) == |queueToSeq(q)|
{
  ReverseLength(q.rear);
}

lemma EnqueueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>, x: T)
  ensures queueToSeq(enqueue(q, x)) == queueToSeq(q) + [x]
  ensures queueSize(enqueue(q, x)) == queueSize(q) + 1
{
  var q' := enqueue(q, x);
  assert q'.front == q.front;
  assert q'.rear == [x] + q.rear;

  ReverseAppend([x], q.rear);
  assert reverse([x]) == [x];
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + reverse([x]);
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + [x];

  calc == {
    queueToSeq(q');
    q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
    q.front + reverse([x] + q.rear);
    q.front + (reverse(q.rear) + [x]);
    { SeqAssoc(q.front, reverse(q.rear), [x]); }
    (q.front + reverse(q.rear)) + [x];
    queueToSeq(q) + [x];
  }

  QueueSizeProperty(q);
  QueueSizeProperty(q');
}

lemma DequeueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures |queueToSeq(q)| > 0
  ensures queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
  ensures queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
{
// Structural induction on q
    match q {
        case Queue(front, rear) => {
            ReverseLength(rear);
            if |front| > 0 {
                // Front is non-empty
                assert queueToSeq(q) == front + reverse(rear);
                assert |queueToSeq(q)| == |front| + |reverse(rear)| == |front| + |rear| > 0;
                assert queueFront(q) == front[0];
                assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == front[0];
                
                var q' := dequeue(q);
                assert q' == Queue(front[1..], rear);
                assert queueToSeq(q') == front[1..] + reverse(rear);
                assert queueToSeq(q)[1..] == (front + reverse(rear))[1..] == front[1..] + reverse(rear);
            } else {
                // Front is empty, rear is non-empty
                assert rear != [];
                assert queueToSeq(q) == [] + reverse(rear) == reverse(rear);
                ReverseLength(rear);
                assert |queueToSeq(q)| == |rear| > 0;
                
                // queueFront returns rear[|rear| - 1]
                ReverseFirst(rear);
                assert reverse(rear)[0] == rear[|rear| - 1];
                assert queueFront(q) == rear[|rear| - 1];
                assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == reverse(rear)[0] == rear[|rear| - 1];
                
                if |rear| == 1 {
                    var q' := dequeue(q);
                    assert q' == Queue([], []);
                    assert queueToSeq(q') == [];
                    assert queueToSeq(q) == reverse(rear);
                    assert |reverse(rear)| == 1;
                    assert queueToSeq(q)[1..] == [];
                } else {
                    var q' := dequeue(q);
                    assert q' == Queue(reverse(rear)[1..], []);
                    assert queueToSeq(q') == reverse(rear)[1..] + reverse([]) == reverse(rear)[1..];
                    assert queueToSeq(q)[1..] == reverse(rear)[1..];
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

lemma SimpleQueueEquivalence<T>(sq: SimpleQueue<T>, q: Queue<T>)
  requires sq.elements == queueToSeq(q)
  ensures simpleQueueIsEmpty(sq) == queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures simpleQueueSize(sq) == queueSize(q)
{
  if queueIsEmpty(q) {
    assert q.front == [] && q.rear == [];
    assert queueToSeq(q) == [];
    assert sq.elements == [];
  }
  QueueSizeProperty(q);
}

  ensures queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
  ensures queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]

function reverse<T>(l: seq<T>): seq<T>
{
  if |l| == 0 then []
  else reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]
}

lemma reverse_permutes<T>(l: seq<T>)
  ensures forall x :: x in l <==> x in reverse(l)
{
  if |l| == 0 {
  } else {
    reverse_permutes(l[1..]);
    forall x
      ensures x in l <==> x in reverse(l)
    {
      if x == l[0] {
        assert x in reverse(l);
      } else {
        assert x in l <==> x in l[1..];
        assert x in l[1..] <==> x in reverse(l[1..]);
        assert x in reverse(l[1..]) ==> x in reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]];
      }
    }
  }
}

lemma reverse_append<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{

}

lemma reverse_involutes<T>(l: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(l)) == l
{
  if |l| == 0 {
  } else {
    calc {
      reverse(reverse(l));
      == reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]);
      == { reverse_append(reverse(l[1..]), [l[0]]); }
      reverse([l[0]]) + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));
      == [l[0]] + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));
      == { reverse_involutes(l[1..]); }
      [l[0]] + l[1..];
      == l;
    }
  }
}

function reverse<T>(l: seq<T>): seq<T>
{
  if |l| == 0 then []
  else reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]
}

lemma reverse_permutes<T>(l: seq<T>)
  ensures forall x :: x in l <==> x in reverse(l)
{
  if |l| == 0 {
  } else {
    reverse_permutes(l[1..]);
    forall x
      ensures x in l <==> x in reverse(l)
    {
      if x == l[0] {
        assert x in reverse(l);
      } else {
        assert x in l <==> x in l[1..];
        assert x in l[1..] <==> x in reverse(l[1..]);
        assert x in reverse(l[1..]) ==> x in reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]];
      }
    }
  }
}

lemma reverse_append<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
// Inductive proof using rule induction
    // following function: reverse
    if (|s1| == 0) {
        assert s1 + s2 == s2;
        assert reverse(s1) == [];
        assert reverse(s2) + [] == reverse(s2);
    } else {
        reverse_append(s1[1..], s2);
        assert s1[1..] + s2 == (s1 + s2)[1..];
        assert (s1 + s2)[0] == s1[0];
        calc {
            reverse(s1 + s2);
            == reverse((s1 + s2)[1..]) + [(s1 + s2)[0]];
            == reverse(s1[1..] + s2) + [s1[0]];
            == { reverse_append(s1[1..], s2); }
            (reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..])) + [s1[0]];
            == reverse(s2) + (reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]]);
            == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1);
        }
    }
}

lemma reverse_involutes<T>(l: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(l)) == l
{
  if |l| == 0 {
  } else {
    calc {
      reverse(reverse(l));
      == reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]);
      == { reverse_append(reverse(l[1..]), [l[0]]); }
      reverse([l[0]]) + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));
      == [l[0]] + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));
      == { reverse_involutes(l[1..]); }
      [l[0]] + l[1..];
      == l;
    }
  }
}

      (reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..])) + [s1[0]];

           reverse(s2) + (reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]]); }

lemma reverse_involutes<T>(l: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(l)) == l
{
// Inductive proof using rule induction
    // following function: reverse
    if (|l| == 0) {
    } else {
        reverse_involutes(l[1..]);
        // We know reverse(reverse(l[1..])) == l[1..] from induction
        
        // reverse(l) == reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]
        // So reverse(reverse(l)) == reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]])
        
        // Use reverse_append to split this
        reverse_append(reverse(l[1..]), [l[0]]);
        // This gives us: reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]) == reverse([l[0]]) + reverse(reverse(l[1..]))
        
        // reverse([l[0]]) == [l[0]]
        assert reverse([l[0]]) == [l[0]];
        
        // reverse(reverse(l[1..])) == l[1..] from induction hypothesis
        // So: reverse(reverse(l)) == [l[0]] + l[1..] == l
        assert [l[0]] + l[1..] == l;
    }
}

proof_dedupCorrect
if (|xs| == 0) {
} else if (xs[0] in dedup(xs[1..])) {
    dedupCorrect(xs[1..]);
    // xs[0] is already in dedup(xs[1..]), so toSet is preserved
    assert xs[0] in toSet(dedup(xs[1..]));
    assert toSet(xs) == {xs[0]} + toSet(xs[1..]);
    assert toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(dedup(xs[1..])) == toSet(xs[1..]);
    assert xs[0] in toSet(xs[1..]);
    assert toSet(xs) == toSet(xs[1..]);
} else {
    dedupCorrect(xs[1..]);
    var rest := dedup(xs[1..]);
    assert noDuplicates(rest);
    assert xs[0] !in rest;
    
    // Show noDuplicates([xs[0]] + rest)
    var result := [xs[0]] + rest;
    
    forall i, j | 0 <= i < j < |result|
        ensures result[i] != result[j]
    {
        if i == 0 {
            // result[0] = xs[0], result[j] is in rest
            assert result[j] == rest[j-1];
            assert result[j] in rest;
            assert xs[0] !in rest;
            assert result[0] != result[j];
        } else {
            // Both i and j are > 0, so we're in rest
            assert result[i] == rest[i-1];
            assert result[j] == rest[j-1];
            assert 0 <= i-1 < j-1 < |rest|;
            assert noDuplicates(rest);
            assert rest[i-1] != rest[j-1];
        }
    }
    
    // Show toSet equality
    assert toSet(xs) == {xs[0]} + toSet(xs[1..]);
    assert toSet(result) == {xs[0]} + toSet(rest);
    assert toSet(rest) == toSet(xs[1..]);
    assert toSet(result) == {xs[0]} + toSet(xs[1..]) == toSet(xs);
}

    // following function: treeToMultiset
    match t {
        case Leaf(v) => {
        }
        case Node(l, r) => {
            flattenCorrect(l);
            flattenCorrect(r);
            toMultisetAppend(flatten(l), flatten(r));
        }
    }
proof_HeapHeightBound
// Inductive proof using rule induction
    // following function: heapHeight
    if (|h.elements| == 0) {
    } else {
        Log2FloorBound(|h.elements|);
        assert log2Floor(|h.elements|) < |h.elements|;
        assert heapHeight(h) == log2Floor(|h.elements|) + 1;
        assert heapHeight(h) <= |h.elements|;
    }
proof_ReverseReverse
// Inductive proof using rule induction
    // following function: reverse
    if (|s| == 0) {
    } else {
        ReverseReverse(s[1..]);
        // reverse(s) == reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]]
        // So reverse(reverse(s)) == reverse(reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]])
        // By ReverseAppend: reverse(a + b) == reverse(b) + reverse(a)
        ReverseAppend(reverse(s[1..]), [s[0]]);
        // reverse(reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]]) == reverse([s[0]]) + reverse(reverse(s[1..]))
        // reverse([s[0]]) == [s[0]]
        // By IH: reverse(reverse(s[1..])) == s[1..]
        // So: reverse(reverse(s)) == [s[0]] + s[1..] == s
        assert reverse([s[0]]) == [s[0]];
        assert [s[0]] + s[1..] == s;
    }
proof_sumDistributive
// Inductive proof using rule induction
    // following function: sum
    if (|xs| == 0) {
    } else {
        sumDistributive(xs[1..], c);
        
        // We need to show that:
        // sum(seq(|xs|, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| => c * xs[i])) == c * sum(xs)
        
        // Let's define the scaled sequence for convenience
        var scaledXs := seq(|xs|, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| => c * xs[i]);
        var scaledTail := seq(|xs[1..]|, i requires 0 <= i < |xs[1..]| => c * xs[1..][i]);
        
        // The inductive hypothesis gives us:
        // sum(scaledTail) == c * sum(xs[1..])
        
        // We need to show scaledXs[1..] == scaledTail
        assert scaledXs[0] == c * xs[0];
        assert |scaledXs| == |xs|;
        assert scaledXs[1..] == scaledTail;
        
        calc {
            sum(scaledXs);
            == scaledXs[0] + sum(scaledXs[1..]);
            == c * xs[0] + sum(scaledTail);
            == { assert sum(scaledTail) == c * sum(xs[1..]); }
            c * xs[0] + c * sum(xs[1..]);
            == c * (xs[0] + sum(xs[1..]));
            == c * sum(xs);
        }
    }
proof_maxIsCorrect
// Inductive proof using rule induction
    // following function: max
    if (|s| == 1) {
    } else {
        var restMax := max(s[1..]);
        maxIsCorrect(s[1..]);
        assert isMax(s[1..], restMax);
        if (s[0] >= restMax) {
            assert max(s) == s[0];
            assert s[0] in s;
            forall x | x in s
                ensures x <= s[0]
            {
                if x == s[0] {
                    assert x <= s[0];
                } else {
                    assert x in s[1..];
                    assert x <= restMax;
                    assert restMax <= s[0];
                }
            }
        } else {
            assert max(s) == restMax;
            assert restMax in s[1..];
            assert restMax in s;
            forall x | x in s
                ensures x <= restMax
            {
                if x == s[0] {
                    assert s[0] < restMax;
                    assert x <= restMax;
                } else {
                    assert x in s[1..];
                    assert x <= restMax;
                }
            }
        }
    }
proof_reverseAppend
match xs {
    case Nil => {
        appendNilRight(reverse(ys));
    }
    case Cons(h, t) => {
        reverseAppend(t, ys);
        appendAssoc(reverse(ys), reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil));
    }
}
proof_reverseReverse
// Inductive proof using rule induction
    // following function: reverse
    match xs {
        case Nil => {
        }
        case Cons(h, t) => {
            reverseReverse(t);
            // reverse(reverse(Cons(h, t)))
            // = reverse(append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil)))
            // = append(reverse(Cons(h, Nil)), reverse(reverse(t)))  by reverseAppend
            // = append(Cons(h, Nil), t)  by induction hypothesis
            // = Cons(h, t)
            reverseAppend(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil));
        }
    }
proof_ReverseAppend
// Inductive proof using rule induction
    // following function: reverse
    if (|s1| == 0) {
        assert s1 + s2 == s2;
        assert reverse(s1) == [];
        assert reverse(s2) + reverse(s1) == reverse(s2) + [] == reverse(s2);
        assert reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1);
    } else {
        ReverseAppend(s1[1..], s2);
        assert s1 == [s1[0]] + s1[1..];
        assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
        assert reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2));
        assert reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2)) == reverse(s1[1..] + s2) + [s1[0]];
        assert reverse(s1[1..] + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..]);
        assert reverse(s1) == reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]];
        SeqAssoc(reverse(s2), reverse(s1[1..]), [s1[0]]);
    }
proof_DequeueCorrect
// Structural induction on q
    match q {
        case Queue(front, rear) => {
            ReverseLength(rear);
            if |front| > 0 {
                // Front is non-empty
                assert queueToSeq(q) == front + reverse(rear);
                assert |queueToSeq(q)| == |front| + |reverse(rear)| == |front| + |rear| > 0;
                assert queueFront(q) == front[0];
                assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == front[0];
                
                var q' := dequeue(q);
                assert q' == Queue(front[1..], rear);
                assert queueToSeq(q') == front[1..] + reverse(rear);
                assert queueToSeq(q)[1..] == (front + reverse(rear))[1..] == front[1..] + reverse(rear);
            } else {
                // Front is empty, rear is non-empty
                assert rear != [];
                assert queueToSeq(q) == [] + reverse(rear) == reverse(rear);
                ReverseLength(rear);
                assert |queueToSeq(q)| == |rear| > 0;
                
                // queueFront returns rear[|rear| - 1]
                ReverseFirst(rear);
                assert reverse(rear)[0] == rear[|rear| - 1];
                assert queueFront(q) == rear[|rear| - 1];
                assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == reverse(rear)[0] == rear[|rear| - 1];
                
                if |rear| == 1 {
                    var q' := dequeue(q);
                    assert q' == Queue([], []);
                    assert queueToSeq(q') == [];
                    assert queueToSeq(q) == reverse(rear);
                    assert |reverse(rear)| == 1;
                    assert queueToSeq(q)[1..] == [];
                } else {
                    var q' := dequeue(q);
                    assert q' == Queue(reverse(rear)[1..], []);
                    assert queueToSeq(q') == reverse(rear)[1..] + reverse([]) == reverse(rear)[1..];
                    assert queueToSeq(q)[1..] == reverse(rear)[1..];
                }
            }
        }
    }
proof_reverse_append
// Inductive proof using rule induction
    // following function: reverse
    if (|s1| == 0) {
        assert s1 + s2 == s2;
        assert reverse(s1) == [];
        assert reverse(s2) + [] == reverse(s2);
    } else {
        reverse_append(s1[1..], s2);
        assert s1[1..] + s2 == (s1 + s2)[1..];
        assert (s1 + s2)[0] == s1[0];
        calc {
            reverse(s1 + s2);
            == reverse((s1 + s2)[1..]) + [(s1 + s2)[0]];
            == reverse(s1[1..] + s2) + [s1[0]];
            == { reverse_append(s1[1..], s2); }
            (reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..])) + [s1[0]];
            == reverse(s2) + (reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]]);
            == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1);
        }
    }
proof_reverse_involutes
// Inductive proof using rule induction
    // following function: reverse
    if (|l| == 0) {
    } else {
        reverse_involutes(l[1..]);
        // We know reverse(reverse(l[1..])) == l[1..] from induction
        
        // reverse(l) == reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]
        // So reverse(reverse(l)) == reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]])
        
        // Use reverse_append to split this
        reverse_append(reverse(l[1..]), [l[0]]);
        // This gives us: reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]) == reverse([l[0]]) + reverse(reverse(l[1..]))
        
        // reverse([l[0]]) == [l[0]]
        assert reverse([l[0]]) == [l[0]];
        
        // reverse(reverse(l[1..])) == l[1..] from induction hypothesis
        // So: reverse(reverse(l)) == [l[0]] + l[1..] == l
        assert [l[0]] + l[1..] == l;
    }
